The object of the game is to predict which slot the ball will land in after the wheel is spun.\r\n- The minimum and maximum bets for the game are displayed on the MIN/MAX section of the table.\r\n- Payouts are made according to the Paytable. When a bet position is highlighted, a window appears and displays the minimum and maximum bet limits for that bet.\r\n- Placing one or several bets. To place a bet, select the chip value and click either a number or a betting position on the table. Click the rebet button to place the same bet as in the previous round.
